Assumptions ^PklyJFtb

1. Using AI driven building (Hack-the-Loyalty), it takes ~15-16 days to get a module designed and deployed to Dev environment.
2. A module is a functional chunk of work (often synonymous with 1-2 small apps/microservices).
3. QA can test full modules in 1 sprint (not tested yet)
4. Bug fixes can be updated and retested in 1 sprint.
5. When Data Design starts for one module, Functional Design can start for another (not tested yet) ^pDQELhTh
